## Environment Variables

Required for development: `DATABASE_URL`, `DIRECT_URL`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY`, `GOOGLE_API_KEY`.

Optional: `FOUNDER_EMAIL` (for daily LinkedIn post emails via `/api/cron/daily-linkedin`).

Conversion / admin: `NEXT_PUBLIC_DEMO_BOOKING_URL` (Calendly link the `BookDemoCTA` component points at; falls back to `/pricing#design-partner` if unset). `ADMIN_USER_IDS` and `ADMIN_EMAILS` gate the admin surfaces (`/dashboard/admin/audit-log`, `/dashboard/admin/monitoring`) and the enterprise-plan bypass.

Encryption + key rotation: `DOCUMENT_ENCRYPTION_KEY` and `SLACK_TOKEN_ENCRYPTION_KEY` (legacy / v1). When rotating, add `DOCUMENT_ENCRYPTION_KEY_V{N}` / `SLACK_TOKEN_ENCRYPTION_KEY_V{N}` and bump `DOCUMENT_ENCRYPTION_KEY_VERSION` / `SLACK_TOKEN_ENCRYPTION_KEY_VERSION` to the new active version. See `src/lib/utils/encryption.ts` header for the full protocol; rotate with `npm run rotate:encryption-key`.

Public demo: `DEMO_USER_ID` — deterministic UUID used as the Document owner for anonymous audits via `/api/demo/run`. MUST also be added to `ADMIN_USER_IDS` so the plan check resolves to enterprise. Rate limits: 1 audit / IP / 24h + 50 audits / day global (~$20/day ceiling). Leave unset to disable the demo endpoint; the UI surfaces a "temporarily unavailable" message.

Sentry source-maps (auto-uploaded post-deploy): `SENTRY_AUTH_TOKEN` is set in Vercel env (Production + Preview). The build script ends with `node scripts/upload-sourcemaps.mjs` which spawns `@sentry/cli` in a fresh process AFTER `next build` finishes — bypasses the webpack-plugin's undici socket leak that caused the 11-hour build hang. No manual upload needed; if `SENTRY_AUTH_TOKEN` is unset, the script logs `[sentry] skipped` and exits 0 (preview deploys without the token still succeed). Generate a token at `https://decision-intel-bu.sentry.io/settings/auth-tokens/` with `project:releases` + `project:write` scopes if it ever needs rotation.

See `.env.example` for the full list with descriptions.

## Bug-prevention tooling (locked 2026-05-01)

Three force multipliers integrated in one batch after the visibility:null incident — turning the "bugs only surface when a user hits them" pattern into "bugs surface at edit time, deploy time, or in a digest PR."

**1. Production observability — `vercel logs --follow` + Sentry auto-upload.** The build script already ends with `node scripts/upload-sourcemaps.mjs` so every Vercel deploy ships symbolicated stack traces (provided `SENTRY_AUTH_TOKEN` is set in Vercel env — Production + Preview). Three new npm shortcuts surface real-time prod errors without copy-paste:

- `npm run vercel:logs` — tail the most-recent deployment in the current project.
- `npm run vercel:logs:prod` — tail production specifically.
- `npm run vercel:logs:errors` — last hour of production logs filtered to error-class lines (matches `error|exception|prismaclient|failed|warn`).

Founder-side one-time actions: (a) keep Vercel CLI current (`pnpm add -g vercel@latest` or `npm i -g vercel@latest`), (b) configure Sentry alert routing in the dashboard so a `PrismaClientValidationError` on a hot path pages your phone instead of just logging.

**2. Compile-time API input validation — `zod-prisma-types`.** New generator block in `prisma/schema.prisma` runs on every `prisma generate`, emitting `src/generated/zod/index.ts` (~93KB single file, ~2,650 lines) with a Zod schema per Prisma model. Lean config — `createInputTypes = false`, `createRelationValuesTypes = false` so we get model-shape schemas only, not the 100s of Create/Update/Where input variants we'd never use. Generated path is gitignored; postinstall regenerates on every `npm install`.

The convention lives at `src/lib/validation/README.md`: every new POST/PATCH route that writes to Prisma derives its input schema from the generated model schema via `.pick()` + `.extend()`. Canonical example at `src/lib/validation/journal.ts` + `src/app/api/journal/route.ts`. When a Prisma field is renamed or its type narrows, `.pick({ field: true })` becomes a TS2322 compile error in the validation file — caught at edit time, not at user-traffic time. Same idea as the Prisma WhereInput tightening on the access helpers, applied to the API boundary.

Forward-looking rule: greenfield routes do NOT hand-write input schemas without referencing the generated schema. The lockstep with Prisma is the whole point. Lazy retrofit on existing routes — fix when you next touch them.

**3. Dependency-drift visibility — Renovate (free via GitHub).** `renovate.json` at repo root configures grouped weekly PRs per ecosystem (react+next+vercel / prisma / supabase / ai providers / sentry / tailwind / test tooling / build+lint). Patches + minors group into one PR per ecosystem; majors land separately with a 7-14 day soak so GitHub surfaces regressions first. Vulnerability alerts bypass the schedule and fire immediately.

Why this matters: yesterday's outage came from a Prisma 7.5 → 7.8 minor-version behavior change (strict WHERE input validation). Renovate's PR description would have surfaced the changelog snippet noting the validation change before it shipped to prod.

Founder-side one-time action: install the Renovate GitHub App at `https://github.com/apps/renovate` — authorize it on the `decision-intel` repo. First run produces a "Configure Renovate" PR that you merge to activate; subsequent runs land grouped weekly digest PRs every Monday at 5am London time. Selected utility libs (date-fns, lodash, uuid, clsx, cva) auto-merge after passing CI; everything else needs review.

Auto-merge guard: `automerge: false` at the top level. Only the explicitly-listed safe utility libs flip to `automerge: true`. Major bumps NEVER auto-merge regardless.

## Git Workflow

- Branch naming: `feature/...`, `fix/...`, `audit/...`
- Commit style: conventional commits (`feat:`, `fix:`, `refactor:`)
- **Always rebase onto main before pushing:** `git fetch origin main && git rebase origin/main` before every push. This keeps history linear and PRs clean. Never push without rebasing first.
- Pre-commit hook runs AI audit (can be slow). Use `--no-verify` only when confident.
- Push with `-u origin <branch>` for new branches.
- CI/CD: GitHub Actions (`.github/workflows/ci-cd.yml`)

## MCP Tools: code-review-graph

This repo has a knowledge graph (~5K nodes / ~39K edges, embeddings built). **Always use the graph before Grep/Glob/Read for code exploration** — faster, cheaper, and returns callers/dependents/test coverage. Graph auto-updates on file changes via the PostToolUse hook. Tool cheatsheet + workflow live in `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md` → "Codebase Awareness".

**Project-specific cautions:**

- `get_architecture_overview` returns ~1.7MB on this repo — it exceeds the tool-result cap and dumps to a file. Start with `list_graph_stats` + `list_communities`; only call the overview if you truly need the full community map, and summarize it via an isolated Agent.
- `query_graph` / `semantic_search_nodes` — always pass `detail_level: "minimal"` and an explicit `limit`.
- General rule for any MCP tool: start with stats/summary, then drill down.
